59:["$","h2",null,{"children":"Sibling AbortController: Cascading Cancellation of Errors"}]
5a:["$","p",null,{"children":"One of the trickiest problems with concurrent execution is error handling. When multiple tools are running in parallel, how should one tool's failure affect the others?"}]
5b:["$","p",null,{"children":["Claude Code's design is: ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"only Bash tool errors cascade-cancel sibling tools"}],". f0:["$","h3",null,{"children":"Why Do Only Bash Errors Cascade?"}]
f1:["$","p",null,{"children":"The code comment says it clearly (lines 357-359):"}]
f2:["$","blockquote",null,{"className":"my-6 border-l-4 border-[var(--accent)] pl-4 text-neutral-300 italic","children":["\n",["$","p",null,{"children":"Bash commands often have implicit dependency chains (e.g. mkdir fails -> subsequent commands pointless). Read/WebFetch/etc are independent — one failure shouldn't nuke the rest."}],"\n"]}]
f3:["$","p",null,{"children":"This is a pragmatic choice. In theory, each tool could declare \"whether my errors should cascade,\" but in practice, only the Bash tool has this kind of implicit dependency relationship. Over-engineering would only increase the cognitive burden on tool developers."}]
f4:["$","h3",null,{"children":"Why Not Support contextModifier for Concurrent Tools?"}]
f5:["$","p",null,{"children":"The code comment (lines 389-390) acknowledges this is a feature gap:"}]
f6:["$","blockquote",null,{"className":"my-6 border-l-4 border-[var(--accent)] pl-4 text-neutral-300 italic","children":["\n",["$","p",null,{"children":"NOTE: we currently don't support context modifiers for concurrent tools. None are actively being used, but if we want to use them in concurrent tools, we need to support that here."}],"\n"]}]
f7:["$","p",null,{"children":"Concurrent tools modifying shared context requires solving race conditions — what happens when two tools simultaneously modify the same context field? The current approach simply prohibits it, waiting for actual demand before designing a solution. This is a textbook application of \"YAGNI\" (You Aren't Gonna Need It)."}]
f8:["$","h3",null,{"children":"Why Does interruptBehavior Default to block?"}]
f9:["$","p",null,{"children":["Because cancelling a write operation midway could cause data corruption. ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"block"}]," means \"let the tool finish,\" which in the worst case only means waiting a few more seconds. ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"cancel"}]," in the worst case could result in a half-written file. Safety > performance."]}]

fb:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"getCompletedResults()"}]," returns a ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"Generator"}],", and ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"getRemainingResults()"}]," returns an ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"AsyncGenerator"}],".
